A genetic investigation of E2A function in lymphocyte development .
Lymphocytes are derived from hematopoietic stem cells ( HSC ) following a series of regulated differentiation events .
Multipotent HSCs become committed to the B cell lineage in bone marrow and the T cell lineage in the thymus after receiving appropriate signals from the corresponding microenvironment .
These committed lymphoid cells must then undergo V ( D ) J recombination at the immunoglobulin:__entity__ gene:__entity__ or T:__entity__ cell:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ gene:__entity__ locus:__entity__ resulting in clonal production of functional B or T lymphocytes , respectively .
Lymphocyte commitment and differentiation are accompanied by programmed gene expression or repression events which are driven by lineage:__entity__ and:__entity__ stage:__entity__ specific:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ .
The basic-helix-loop-helix:__entity__ (:__entity__ bHLH:__entity__ ):__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ encoded by the E2A:__entity__ gene:__entity__ are involved in several differentiation events during B and T cell development , including lineage commitment , initiation of V ( D ) J recombination , and antigen receptor mediated proliferation and differentiation .
Several recent reviews have provided a comprehensive discussion of biochemical , cellular , and genetic research on E2A function in lymphocyte development ( 1 , 2 ) .
Here , we only discuss some of the genetic approaches our laboratory ( except where it is noted ) has undertaken to investigate the molecular pathways mediated by E2A:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ in lymphocyte development
D609 inhibits ionizing radiation-induced oxidative damage by acting as a potent antioxidant .
Tricyclodecan-9-yl-xanthogenate ( D609 ) has been extensively studied in biological systems and exhibits a variety of biological functions , including antiviral , antitumor , and anti-inflammatory activities .
Most of these activities have been largely attributed to the inhibitory effect of D609 on phosphatidylcholine-specific phospholipase:__entity__ C:__entity__ .
However , as a xanthate derivative , D609 is a strong electrolyte and readily dissociates to xanthate anions and cations of alkali metals in solution .
Xanthate anions and protonated xanthic acid contain a free thiol moiety and are highly reductive .
This implies that D609 and other xanthate derivatives may function as potent antioxidants .
Indeed , we found that D609 inhibited the Fenton reaction-induced oxidation of dihydrorhodamine 123 in a dose-dependent manner similar to that of pyrrolidinedithiocarbamate , a well known antioxidant .
In addition , D609 inhibited the formation of the alpha-phenyl-tert-butylnitrone-free radical spin adducts and lipid peroxidation of synaptosomal membranes by the Fenton reagents .
Furthermore , preincubation of lymphocytes with D609 resulted in a significant diminution of ionizing radiation ( IR ) -induced 1 ) production of reactive oxygen species ; 2 ) decrease in intracellular reduced glutathione ; 3 ) oxidative damage to proteins and lipids ; and 4 ) activation of nuclear:__entity__ factor-kappaB:__entity__ .
Moreover , when D609 ( 50 mg/kg i.v. ) was administered to mice 10 min prior to total body IR ( 6.5 and 8.5 Gy ) , it protected the mice from IR-induced lethality .
Thus , these results indicate that D609 is a potent antioxidant and has the ability to inhibit IR-induced cellular oxidative stress .
Inhibition of AP-1:__entity__ by the glucocorticoid-inducible protein:__entity__ GILZ:__entity__ .
The immunosuppressive effects of glucocorticoids arise largely by inhibition of cytokine gene expression , which has been ascribed to interference between the glucocorticoid:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ and transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ such as AP-1:__entity__ and NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ as well as by competition for common coactivators .

This could be accounted for by GILZ:__entity__ -mediated inhibition of Egr-2:__entity__ and Egr-3:__entity__ , NFAT/AP-1:__entity__ -inducible transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ that bind a regulatory:__entity__ element:__entity__ in the FasL:__entity__ promoter:__entity__ and up-regulate FasL expression .
GILZ:__entity__ also potently inhibited AP-1-driven:__entity__ and:__entity__ IL-2:__entity__ promoter-driven:__entity__ reporter:__entity__ constructs:__entity__ , and recombinant GILZ:__entity__ specifically interacted with c-Fos:__entity__ and c-Jun:__entity__ in vitro and inhibited the binding of active:__entity__ AP-1:__entity__ to its target DNA .
Whereas homodimerization of GILZ:__entity__ required the presence of its leucine:__entity__ zipper:__entity__ , the interaction with c-Fos:__entity__ and c-Jun:__entity__ occurred through the N-terminal:__entity__ 60-amino:__entity__ acid:__entity__ region:__entity__ of GILZ:__entity__ .
Thus , GILZ:__entity__ represents a glucocorticoid-induced gene product that can inhibit a variety of activation-induced events , at least in part by direct interference with AP-1:__entity__ , and is therefore a candidate for a mediator of glucocorticoid-induced immunosuppression .
Pharmacokinetic differences between a T cell-tolerizing and a T cell-activating peptide .
Vaccination with a peptide representing a CTL epitope from the human papillomavirus ( HPV ) 16 E7:__entity__ protein:__entity__ induces a specific CTL response that prevents the outgrowth of HPV16 E7-expressing tumors .
In contrast , vaccination with a peptide encoding an adenovirus type 5 ( Ad5 ) E1A CTL epitope results in CTL tolerance and enhanced growth of an Ad5 E1A-expressing tumor .
It is unclear why these peptides induce such opposite effects .
To determine whether a difference in pharmacokinetics can explain the functional contrasts , tritiated Ad5 E1A and HPV16 E7 peptides were injected into mice .
Results show that the tolerizing peptide spread through the body 16 times faster than the activating peptide and was cleared at least 2 times faster .
The HPV16 E7 peptide kinetics correlated with the kinetics of HPV16:__entity__ E7:__entity__ -specific CTL induction .
In contrast , Ad5 E1A peptide injection resulted in physical deletion of preexisting Ad5:__entity__ E1A:__entity__ -specific CTLs:__entity__ within 24 h after injection .
This tolerization occurred at the time when the peptide reached its maximum peptide concentration in the organs .
These data suggest that ubiquitous expression of the tolerizing Ad5 E1A peptide within a short period of time causes activation-induced cell death of Ad5:__entity__ E1A:__entity__ -specific CTLs:__entity__ .
Therefore , information on the pharmacokinetics of peptides is vital for the safety and efficacy of peptide-based vaccines .

Human:__entity__ ACAT-1:__entity__ gene:__entity__ contains two promoters:__entity__ ( P1:__entity__ and P7:__entity__ ) , each located in a different chromosome:__entity__ (:__entity__ 1:__entity__ and:__entity__ 7:__entity__ ):__entity__ ( Li , B. L. , Li , X. L. , Duan , Z. J. , Lee , O. , Lin , S. , Ma , Z. M. , Chang , C. C. , Yang , X. Y. , Park , J. P. , Mohandas , T. K. , Noll , W. , Chan , L. , and Chang , T. Y. ( 1999 ) J. Biol Chem. 274 , 11060-11071 ) .
Interferon-gamma:__entity__ ( IFN-gamma:__entity__ ) , a cytokine:__entity__ that exerts many pro-atherosclerotic effects in vivo , causes up-regulation of ACAT-1:__entity__ mRNA:__entity__ in human blood monocyte-derived macrophages and macrophage-like cells but not in other cell types .

Inhaled nitric oxide down-regulates intrapulmonary nitric oxide production in lipopolysaccharide-induced acute lung injury .
OBJECTIVE : To examine whether inhaled nitric oxide ( NO ) affected the intrapulmonary production of NO , reactive oxygen species , and nuclear:__entity__ factor-kappaB:__entity__ in a lipopolysaccharide ( LPS ) -induced model of acute lung injury .
DESIGN : Prospective , randomized , laboratory study .
SETTING : Experimental laboratory at a biomedical institute .
SUBJECTS : Twenty male rabbits weighing 2.5-3.5 kg .
INTERVENTIONS : Saline or LPS ( 5 mg/kg of body weight ) was administered intravenously with or without NO inhalation ( 10 ppm ) in each group of five rabbits .
MEASUREMENTS AND MAIN RESULTS : LPS increased the lung leak index , the neutrophils and NO levels in bronchoalveolar lavage fluid , and NO levels produced by resting and stimulated alveolar macrophages .
Inhaled NO decreased the lung leak index , the neutrophils and NO levels as measured by nitrite levels in the lavage fluid , and NO produced by the resting and stimulated alveolar macrophages .
Inhaled NO also blocked the activities of reactive oxygen species and nuclear:__entity__ factor-kappaB:__entity__ binding to DNA in lavage cells and in alveolar macrophages .
CONCLUSION : Inhaled NO attenuates LPS-induced acute lung injury , possibly by decreasing NO production in the lungs .
The mechanism of reducing NO production resulting from inhaled NO may involve , in part , the activities of reactive oxygen species and/or nuclear:__entity__ factor-kappaB:__entity__ .
Treatment of allergic airway inflammation and hyperresponsiveness by antisense-induced local blockade of GATA-3:__entity__ expression .
Recent studies in transgenic mice have revealed that expression of a dominant negative form of the transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ GATA-3:__entity__ in T cells can prevent T helper cell type 2 ( Th2 ) -mediated allergic airway inflammation in mice .
However , it remains unclear whether GATA-3:__entity__ plays a role in the effector phase of allergic airway inflammation and whether antagonizing the expression and/or function of GATA-3:__entity__ can be used for the therapy of allergic airway inflammation and hyperresponsiveness .
Here , we analyzed the effects of locally antagonizing GATA-3:__entity__ function in a murine model of asthma .
We could suppress GATA-3 expression in interleukin:__entity__ (:__entity__ IL:__entity__ ):__entity__ -4:__entity__ -producing T cells in vitro and in vivo by an antisense phosphorothioate oligonucleotide overlapping the translation:__entity__ start:__entity__ site:__entity__ of GATA-3:__entity__ , whereas nonsense control oligonucleotides were virtually inactive .
In a murine model of asthma associated with allergic pulmonary inflammation and hyperresponsiveness in ovalbumin ( OVA ) -sensitized mice , local intranasal administration of fluorescein isothiocyanate-labeled GATA-3 antisense oligonucleotides led to DNA uptake in lung cells associated with a reduction of intracellular GATA-3 expression .
Such intrapulmonary blockade of GATA-3 expression caused an abrogation of signs of lung inflammation including infiltration of eosinophils and Th2 cytokine production .
Furthermore , treatment with antisense but not nonsense oligonucleotides induced a significant reduction of airway hyperresponsiveness in OVA-sensitized mice to levels comparable to saline-treated control mice , as assessed by both enhanced pause ( PenH ) responses and pulmonary resistance determined by body plethysmography .
These data indicate a critical role for GATA-3:__entity__ in the effector phase of a murine asthma model and suggest that local delivery of GATA-3 antisense oligonucleotides may be a novel approach for the treatment of airway hyperresponsiveness such as in asthma .
This approach has the potential advantage of suppressing the expression of various proinflammatory:__entity__ Th2:__entity__ cytokines:__entity__ simultaneously rather than suppressing the activity of a single cytokine:__entity__ .
T helper-cell phenotype regulates atherosclerosis in mice under conditions of mild hypercholesterolemia .
BACKGROUND : T cells are implicated in atherosclerosis , but little is known about the genetic control or molecular pathways , especially under conditions of mild hypercholesterolemia .
METHODS AND RESULTS : BALB/c mice , making a CD4+ Th2 ( IL-4+ ) cell response , express both MHC:__entity__ class:__entity__ II:__entity__ antigens:__entity__ ( IA:__entity__ (:__entity__ d:__entity__ ):__entity__ , IE:__entity__ (:__entity__ d:__entity__ ):__entity__ ) and are atherosclerosis-resistant .

To evaluate T helper-cell phenotype in fatty streak formation , wild-type C57Bl/6 mice ( IA ( b ) +IE- ) and transgenic mice , either AB ( o ) , IA ( b ) -IE- ; ABEalpha , IA-IE ( k ) + ; or BL : TG : Ealpha , IA ( b ) +IE ( k ) + , were fed a high-cholesterol diet for 16 weeks and evaluated histomorphometrically for aortic lesions .
Lesion size in AB ( o ) , ABEalpha , and BL : TG : Ealpha strains was decreased by 54 % , 79 % , and 82 % , respectively , compared with wild-type , correlating with decreased Th1 and increased Th2 expression and suggesting that T helper-cell phenotype is important in fatty lesion development .
Decreasing Th1 cells by antibodies:__entity__ ( alpha-CD4:__entity__ ) or cytokines:__entity__ ( IL-4:__entity__ ) also caused > /=80 % reductions in lesion size .

CONCLUSIONS : In mildly hypercholesterolemic C57Bl/6 mice , presence of IA:__entity__ (:__entity__ b:__entity__ ):__entity__ and absence of IE:__entity__ regulated CD4+ T helper-cell phenotype ; fatty lesions were proportional to IFNgamma+ Th1 cells in both C57Bl/6 and BALB/c strains .
IFN-gamma:__entity__ may participate through macrophage activation , whereas IL-4:__entity__ may act to limit Th1-cell response .
Requirement for p38:__entity__ and p44/p42:__entity__ mitogen-activated:__entity__ protein:__entity__ kinases:__entity__ in RAGE:__entity__ -mediated nuclear:__entity__ factor-kappaB:__entity__ transcriptional activation and cytokine secretion .

Antigen-receptor cross-linking and lipopolysaccharide trigger distinct phosphoinositide:__entity__ 3-kinase:__entity__ -dependent pathways to NF-kappa B activation in primary B cells .
The NF-kappaB/Rel:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ play an important role in the expression of genes involved in B cell development , differentiation and function .
Nuclear:__entity__ NF-kappaB:__entity__ is induced in B cells by engagement of either the BCR:__entity__ or CD40:__entity__ or by stimulation with lipopolysaccharide ( LPS ) .

Tetramer-guided epitope mapping : rapid identification and characterization of immunodominant CD4+ T cell epitopes from complex antigens:__entity__ .
T cell responses to Ags:__entity__ involve recognition of selected peptide:__entity__ epitopes:__entity__ contained within the antigenic:__entity__ protein:__entity__ .

By using tetramers:__entity__ to sort individual cells , we easily obtained a large number of clones specific to these epitopes:__entity__ .
Although DRA1*0101/DRB1*0401 and DRA1*0101/DRB1*0404 are structurally very similar , nonoverlapping VP16:__entity__ epitopes:__entity__ were identified , illustrating high selectivity of individual allele polymorphisms within common MHC variants .

Localized pancreatic NF-kappaB activation and inflammatory response in taurocholate-induced pancreatitis .
Transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ nuclear:__entity__ factor-kappaB:__entity__ ( NF-kappaB:__entity__ ) is activated in cerulein pancreatitis and mediates cytokine expression .
The role of transcription factor activation in other models of pancreatitis has not been established .
Here we report upregulation of NF-kappaB:__entity__ and inflammatory:__entity__ molecules:__entity__ , and their correlation with local pancreatic injury , in a model of severe pancreatitis .

Saline infusion mildly affected these parameters .
AP-1:__entity__ was strongly activated in both pancreatic segments after either taurocholate or saline infusion .
NF-kappaB:__entity__ inhibition with N-acetylcysteine ameliorated the local inflammatory response .
Correlation between localized NF-kappaB:__entity__ activation , cytokine upregulation , and tissue damage suggests a key role for NF-kappaB:__entity__ in the development of the inflammatory response of acute pancreatitis .
CD45:__entity__ tyrosine:__entity__ phosphatase:__entity__ controls common gamma-chain:__entity__ cytokine:__entity__ -mediated STAT:__entity__ and extracellular signal-related kinase phosphorylation in activated human lymphoblasts : inhibition of proliferation without induction of apoptosis .
The objective of this study was to test whether CD45 signals can influence signaling processes in activated human lymphoblasts .
To this end , we generated lymphoblasts which proliferate in response to common gamma-chain:__entity__ cytokines:__entity__ , but readily undergo apoptosis after cytokine withdrawal .
In experiments with the CD45R0:__entity__ mAb:__entity__ UCHL-1:__entity__ , but not control:__entity__ CD45:__entity__ mAbs:__entity__ , we found significant inhibition of proliferation .

Addition of CD3:__entity__ mAb:__entity__ OKT-3:__entity__ had no influence on IL-2-mediated proliferation ( with or without UCHL-1:__entity__ ) .
In contrast , after addition of OKT-3:__entity__ to IL-4:__entity__ - and IL-7:__entity__ -stimulated proliferation assays , UCHL-1:__entity__ signals could not significantly alter cellular proliferation .
We did not find induction of apoptosis following CD45R0 signaling .

In conclusion , we illustrate that CD45R0 signals control early cytokine receptor-associated signaling processes and mRNA and DNA synthesis in activated human lymphoblasts .
Furthermore , we show the existence of CD45:__entity__ epitopes:__entity__ ( GAP8.3:__entity__ ) , which are active and critical for signaling in quiescent lymphocytes , but are nonfunctional in activated human lymphoblasts .
Pax5:__entity__ determines the identity of B cells from the beginning to the end of B-lymphopoiesis .
Despite being one of the most intensively studied cell types , the molecular basis of B cell specification is largely unknown .
The Pax5:__entity__ gene:__entity__ encoding the transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ BSAP:__entity__ is required for progression of B-lymphopoiesis beyond the pro-B cell stage .
Pax5-deficient pro-B cells are , however , not yet committed to the B-lymphoid lineage , but instead have a broad lymphomyeloid developmental potential .
Pax5:__entity__ appears to mediate B-lineage commitment by repressing the transcription of non-B-lymphoid:__entity__ genes:__entity__ and by simultaneously activating the expression of B-lineage-specific:__entity__ genes:__entity__ .
Pax5:__entity__ thus functions both as a transcriptional repressor and activator , depending on its interactions with corepressors:__entity__ of the Groucho:__entity__ protein:__entity__ family:__entity__ or with positive regulators such as the TATA-binding:__entity__ protein:__entity__ .
Once committed to the B-lineage , B cells require Pax5:__entity__ function to maintain their B-lymphoid identity throughout B cell development
Partners in transcription : NFAT:__entity__ and AP-1:__entity__ .
Combinatorial regulation is a powerful mechanism that enables tight control of gene expression , via integration of multiple signaling pathways that induce different transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ required for enhanceosome assembly .
The four calcium-regulated transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ of the NFAT:__entity__ family:__entity__ act synergistically with AP-1:__entity__ (:__entity__ Fos/Jun:__entity__ ):__entity__ proteins:__entity__ on composite DNA elements which contain adjacent NFAT:__entity__ and:__entity__ AP-1:__entity__ binding:__entity__ sites:__entity__ , where they form highly stable ternary complexes to regulate the expression of diverse inducible genes .
Concomitant induction of NFAT:__entity__ and AP-1:__entity__ requires concerted activation of two different signaling pathways : calcium/calcineurin , which promotes NFAT dephosphorylation , nuclear translocation and activation ; and protein:__entity__ kinase:__entity__ C:__entity__ (:__entity__ PKC:__entity__ ):__entity__ /Ras:__entity__ , which promotes the synthesis , phosphorylation and activation of members of the Fos:__entity__ and:__entity__ Jun:__entity__ families:__entity__ of transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ .
A fifth member of the NFAT:__entity__ family:__entity__ , NFAT5:__entity__ , controls the cellular response to osmotic stress , by a mechanism that requires dimer formation and is independent of calcineurin:__entity__ or of interaction with AP-1:__entity__ .
Pharmacological interference with theNFAT : AP-1 interaction may be useful in selective manipulation of the immune response .
Balanced activation of NFAT:__entity__ and AP-1:__entity__ is known to be required for productive immune responses , but the role of NFAT : AP-1 interactions in other cell types and biological processes remains to be understood .
Cytokine production by Vgamma ( + ) -T-cell subsets is an important factor determining CD4 ( + ) -Th-cell phenotype and susceptibility of BALB/c mice to coxsackievirus B3-induced myocarditis .
Two coxsackievirus B3 ( CVB3 ) variants ( H3 and H310A1 ) differ by a single amino acid mutation in the VP2:__entity__ capsid:__entity__ protein:__entity__ .
H3 induces severe myocarditis in BALB/c mice , but H310A1 is amyocarditic .
Infection with H3 , but not H310A1 , preferentially activates Vgamma4 Vdelta4 cells , which are strongly positive for gamma:__entity__ interferon:__entity__ ( IFN-gamma:__entity__ ) , whereas Vgamma1 Vdelta4 cells are increased in both H3 and H310A1 virus-infected animals .

Depleting Vgamma4 ( + ) cells suppressed myocarditis and reduced CD4 ( + ) IFN-gamma ( + ) cells but increased CD4 ( + ) IL-4 ( + ) T cells .
The role of cytokine production by Vgamma1 ( + ) and Vgamma4 ( + ) T cells was investigated by adoptively transferring these cells isolated from H3-infected BALB/c Stat4 knockout ( Stat4ko ) ( defective in IFN-gamma:__entity__ expression ) or BALB/c Stat6ko ( defective in IL-4 expression ) mice into H3 virus-infected wild-type BALB/c recipients .
Vgamma4 and Vgamma1 ( + ) T cells from Stat4ko mice expressed IL-4:__entity__ but no or minimal IFN-gamma:__entity__ , whereas these cell populations derived from Stat6ko mice expressed IFN-gamma:__entity__ but no IL-4:__entity__ .
Stat4ko Vgamma1 ( + ) cells ( IL-4 ( + ) ) suppress myocarditis .
Stat6ko Vgamma1 ( + ) cells ( IFN-gamma ( + ) ) were not inhibitory .
Stat6ko Vgamma4 ( + ) cells ( IFN-gamma ( + ) ) significantly enhanced myocarditis .
Stat4ko Vgamma4 ( + ) cells ( IL-4 ( + ) ) neither inhibited nor enhanced disease .
These results show that distinct gammadelta-T-cell subsets control myocarditis susceptibility and bias the CD4 ( + ) -Th-cell response .
The cytokines:__entity__ produced by the Vgamma subpopulation have a significant influence on the CD4:__entity__ ( + ) -Th-cell phenotype .

These findings further substantiate the role of plasmin:__entity__ as a proinflammatory activator of human monocytes and reveal an important new link between the plasminogen-plasmin system and inflammation .

STAT3:__entity__ is constitutively active in some patients with Polycythemia rubra vera .
OBJECTIVE : Polycythemia vera is a clonal stem cell disorder characterized by hyperproliferation of the erythroid , myeloid , and megakaryocytic lineages .
While it has been shown that progenitor cells of P. vera patients are hypersensitive to several growth factors including erythropoietin:__entity__ , insulin-like:__entity__ growth:__entity__ factor-1:__entity__ , thrombopoietin:__entity__ , interleukin-3:__entity__ , and granulocyte/monocyte:__entity__ colony-stimulating:__entity__ factor:__entity__ , the molecular pathogenesis of this disease remains unknown .
Growth factor hypersensitivity could be mediated by changes in signal transduction pathways .
We therefore investigated a common downstream effector of cytokines:__entity__ , the signal:__entity__ transducers:__entity__ and:__entity__ activators:__entity__ of:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ ( STATs:__entity__ ) .
A constitutive activation of STAT:__entity__ factors:__entity__ could explain the increased proliferation of P. vera cells even in the absence of growth factor stimulation .
METHODS : Peripheral granulocytes from patients with P. vera and from healthy volunteers were assayed for STAT1:__entity__ ,:__entity__ 3:__entity__ ,:__entity__ and:__entity__ 5:__entity__ DNA binding by electrophoretic mobility shift assay .
RESULTS : Four of 14 P. vera patients analyzed showed constitutive STAT3 DNA binding in unstimulated peripheral granulocytes , while none of the 17 healthy volunteers tested did .
None of the subjects showed constitutive STAT1:__entity__ or STAT5:__entity__ activity .
Western blotting demonstrated that , in the three patients , STAT3:__entity__ is constitutively phosphorylated on Tyr 705 , whereas it is unphosphorylated in the other patients and in controls .
Interestingly , constitutive STAT3:__entity__ activity did not correlate with the duration of disease or the treatment regimen .
It was observed in a recently diagnosed patient and in two patients treated only with phlebotomy .
CONCLUSION : Our data suggest that constitutive phosphorylation and activation of STAT3:__entity__ is not a secondary event induced by mutagenizing agents or by prolonged hyperproliferation of hematopoietic cells , but rather represents a primary molecular aberration .
Constitutively:__entity__ active:__entity__ STAT3:__entity__ may contribute to the growth factor hypersensitivity of P. vera cells .
Identification of phosphorylation:__entity__ sites:__entity__ for Bruton:__entity__ 's:__entity__ tyrosine:__entity__ kinase:__entity__ within the transcriptional:__entity__ regulator:__entity__ BAP/TFII-I:__entity__ .
Bruton:__entity__ 's:__entity__ tyrosine:__entity__ kinase:__entity__ ( Btk:__entity__ ) , a member of the Tec:__entity__ family:__entity__ of:__entity__ cytosolic:__entity__ kinases:__entity__ , is essential for B cell development and function .
BAP/TFII-I:__entity__ , a protein implicated in transcriptional regulation , is associated with Btk:__entity__ in B cells and is transiently phosphorylated on tyrosine following B cell receptor engagement .
BAP/TFII-I:__entity__ is a substrate for Btk:__entity__ in vitro and is hyperphosphorylated on tyrosine upon coexpression with Btk:__entity__ in mammalian cells .
In an effort to understand the physiologic consequences of BAP/TFII-I:__entity__ tyrosine phosphorylation following B cell receptor stimulation , site-directed mutagenesis and phosphopeptide mapping were used to locate the predominant sites of BAP/TFII-I:__entity__ phosphorylation by Btk:__entity__ in vitro .
These residues , Tyr248 , Tyr357 , and Tyr462 , were also found to be the major sites for Btk:__entity__ -dependent phosphorylation of BAP/TFII-I:__entity__ in vivo .
Residues Tyr357 and Tyr462 are contained within the loop:__entity__ regions:__entity__ of adjacent helix-loop-helix-like:__entity__ repeats:__entity__ within BAP/TFII-I:__entity__ .

Distinct BMI-1:__entity__ and EZH2:__entity__ expression patterns in thymocytes and mature T cells suggest a role for Polycomb:__entity__ genes:__entity__ in human T cell differentiation .
BMI-1:__entity__ and EZH2:__entity__ Polycomb-group:__entity__ (:__entity__ PcG:__entity__ ):__entity__ proteins:__entity__ belong to two distinct protein complexes involved in the regulation of hematopoiesis .
Using unique PcG-specific antisera and triple immunofluorescence , we found that mature resting peripheral T cells expressed BMI-1:__entity__ , whereas dividing blasts were EZH2 ( + ) .
By contrast , subcapsular immature double-negative ( DN ) ( CD4 ( - ) /CD8 ( - ) ) T cells in the thymus coexpressed BMI-1:__entity__ and EZH2:__entity__ or were BMI-1 single positive .
Their descendants , double-positive ( DP ; CD4 ( + ) /CD8 ( + ) ) cortical thymocytes , expressed EZH2:__entity__ without BMI-1:__entity__ .
Most EZH2 ( + ) DN and DP thymocytes were dividing , while DN BMI-1 ( + ) /EZH2 ( - ) thymocytes were resting and proliferation was occasionally noted in DN BMI-1 ( + ) /EZH2 ( + ) cells .
Maturation of DP cortical thymocytes to single-positive ( CD4 ( + ) /CD8 ( - ) or CD8 ( + ) /CD4 ( - ) ) medullar thymocytes correlated with decreased detectability of EZH2:__entity__ and continued relative absence of BMI-1:__entity__ .
Our data show that BMI-1:__entity__ and EZH2:__entity__ expression in mature peripheral T cells is mutually exclusive and linked to proliferation status , and that this pattern is not yet established in thymocytes of the cortex and medulla .

They probably reflect stabilization of cell type-specific gene expression and irreversibility of lineage choice .
The difference in PcG expression between medullar thymocytes and mature interfollicular T cells indicates that additional maturation processes occur after thymocyte transportation from the thymus .
Stepwise lineage restriction of progenitors in lympho-myelopoiesis .
It has long been controversial whether hematopoiesis progresses through ordered stages of determination as in embryonic development .
This is due to the absence of a methodology capable of exactly determining the developmental potential of hematopoietic stem/progenitor cells .
The multilineage progenitor ( MLP ) assay enabled us to discriminate among seven types of hematopoietic progenitors , which are multipotent progenitor p-MTB ( capable of generating myeloid , T and B cells ) , bipotent progenitors p-MT , p-MB and p-TB , and unipotent progenitors p-M , p-T and p-B .
Among these seven types , the p-TB type progenitor was found to be absent .
These findings indicate that the process of lineage commitment proceeds through an ordered but not random process .
By extending the area of investigation to include the erythroid lineage , more convincing evidence for the ordered process was obtained .
Detailed and exact illustration of the process of hematopoiesis will provide an opportunity to revive hematopoiesis as one of the most fascinating targets of research in developmental biology
Epstein-Barr Virus and its glycoprotein-350:__entity__ upregulate IL-6:__entity__ in human B-lymphocytes via CD21:__entity__ , involving activation of NF-kappaB:__entity__ and different signaling pathways .
Epstein-Barr virus ( EBV ) is a ubiquitous and highly immunotropic gamma herpesvirus that infects more than 90 % of humans worldwide .
Its pathogenicity leads to a number of diseases including tumors that result from EBV 's ability to readily transform B-lymphocytes and , to a lesser extent , epithelial cells .
EBV utilizes CD21/CR2:__entity__ as its receptor on B cells to initiate the infection process .
EBV binds to CR2:__entity__ through its major:__entity__ envelope:__entity__ glycoprotein-350:__entity__ ( gp350:__entity__ ) and is also a remarkable immunomodulating agent .
We had previously shown that EBV is capable of modulating the synthesis of a number of cytokines:__entity__ .
We now show that while both purified recombinant:__entity__ gp350:__entity__ ( rgp350:__entity__ ) and EBV upregulate IL-6:__entity__ mRNA:__entity__ synthesis in B cells , EBV-induced IL-6 gene activation occurs for a significantly longer period of time ( i.e. 12 hours for EBV as compared to 6 hours for rgp350:__entity__ ) .
Moreover , the half-life of EBV-induced IL-6:__entity__ mRNA:__entity__ was also significantly longer ( 10 hours ) than that of mRNA induced by rgp350:__entity__ ( about 6 hours ) .
Both EBV and gp350:__entity__ enhance the binding of the NF-kappaB:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ , as determined by band-shift and augment NF-kappaB:__entity__ -mediated activation of a CAT:__entity__ reporter:__entity__ plasmid:__entity__ .
Furthermore , we demonstrate that while the activation of IL-6 gene expression by gp350:__entity__ is mediated primarily by the protein kinase C pathway , EBV can mediate its effects through multiple signaling pathways .
To our knowledge this is the first report showing that the binding of a herpesvirus:__entity__ envelope:__entity__ glycoprotein:__entity__ to CR2:__entity__ on human B cells results in the activation of the NF-kappaB:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ leading to the upregulation of IL-6 gene expression in these lymphocytes .

Gene- and tissue-specificity of mutation in Big Blue rats treated with the hepatocarcinogen N-hydroxy-2-acetylaminofluorene .
In a previous study , we found that treating transgenic Big Blue rats with the hepatocarcinogen N-hydroxy-2-acetylaminofluorene ( N-OH-AAF ) produced the same major DNA adduct in the target liver and the nontarget spleen lymphocytes and bone marrow cells , induced lacI mutants in the liver , and induced much lower frequencies of l acI and hprt mutants in spleen lymphocytes .
In the present study , sequence analysis was conducted on lacI:__entity__ DNA:__entity__ and hprt:__entity__ cDNA:__entity__ from the mutants , to determine the mutational specificity of N-OH-AAF in the rat .
All the mutation spectra from N-OH-AAF-treated rats differed significantly from corresponding mutation profiles from untreated animals ( P = 0.02 to P < 0.0001 ) .
Although there were similarities among the mutational patterns derived from N-OH-AAF-treated rats ( e.g. , G : C -- > T : A transversion was the most common mutation in all mutation sets ) , there were significant differences in the patterns of basepair substitution and frameshift mutation between the liver and spleen lymphocyte lacI mutants ( P = 0.02 ) and between the spleen lymphocyte lacI and hprt mutants ( P = 0.04 ) .
Also , multiplex PCR analysis of genomic:__entity__ DNA:__entity__ from the hprt mutants indicated that 12 % of mutants from treated rats had major deletions in the hprt:__entity__ gene:__entity__ ; no corresponding incidence of large deletions was evident among lacI mutations .
All the mutation profiles reflect the general mutational specificity of the major DNA adduct formed by N-OH-AAF .
The differences between N-OH-AAF mutation in the endogenous:__entity__ gene:__entity__ and transgene:__entity__ can be partially explained by the structures of the two genes .
The tissue-specificity of the mutation spectra may contribute to targeting tumor formation to the liver .

Regulation of cytokine production in T-cell responses to inhalant allergen : GATA-3:__entity__ expression distinguishes between Th1- and Th2-polarized immunity .
BACKGROUND : The precise nature of allergen-specific cytokine responses in atopics versus non-atopics , in particular the 'Th1 polarity ' of responses in non-atopics , remains controversial .
This is due in part to the relative insensitivity of cytokine detection systems , and associated variations in kinetics of cytokine production and catabolism in in vitro culture systems .
As an alternative to cytokine measurement , this study focuses on expression of the transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ GATA-3:__entity__ for analysis of allergen-specific Th cell responses .
METHODS : Cord blood mononuclear cells were Th1- or Th2-polarized by culture in IL-12- or IL-4-employing established methods ; PBMC from house dust mite ( HDM ) -sensitive atopics and controls were stimulated overnight with HDM ; cytokine production was measured by ELISA and GATA-3:__entity__ mRNA:__entity__ expression by PCR .
RESULTS : Cytokine:__entity__ -driven Th2 polarization of naive T cells is associated with marked upregulation of GATA-3:__entity__ expression , whereas a reciprocal expression pattern accompanies differentiation towards the Th1 cytokine phenotype .
In T cells from HDM skin prick test-positive ( HDM-SPT+/HDM-IgE+ ) volunteers , overnight stimulation results in marked upregulation of GATA-3:__entity__ expression , compared to an equally marked downregulation of expression in T cells from SPT-/IgE- subjects .
In subjects who are HDM-SPT+ but IgE- , GATA-3:__entity__ expression levels remained relatively stable during culture with HDM .
CONCLUSIONS : Upregulation of GATA-3:__entity__ expression in PBMC is a hallmark of the early phase of Th2 recall responses to specific allergen in atopics .
The reciprocal expression pattern observed in HDM-specific recall responses of non-atopics provides independent confirmation of the presence of underlying Th1-like immunity in these subjects .
The parallel findings in neonatal T cells suggest that the same approach may be utilized for monitoring the progress of allergen-specific Th1/Th2 memory development during early childhood , and hence in assessment of risk for future allergic disease .

The heat shock response reduces myelin:__entity__ oligodendrocyte:__entity__ glycoprotein:__entity__ -induced experimental autoimmune encephalomyelitis in mice .
The stress response ( SR ) can block inflammatory gene expression by preventing activation of transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ nuclear:__entity__ factor-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ ( NF-kappaB:__entity__ ) .

The HSR reduced the incidence of EAE by 70 % , delayed disease onset by 6 days , and attenuated disease severity .
The HSR attenuated leukocyte infiltration into CNS assessed by quantitation of perivascular infiltrates , and by reduced staining for CD4:__entity__ and CD25:__entity__ immunopositive T-cells .
T-cell activation , assessed by the production of interferon:__entity__ gamma:__entity__ ( IFNgamma:__entity__ ) in response to MOG:__entity__ (:__entity__ 35-55:__entity__ ):__entity__ , was also decreased by the HSR .
The HSR reduced inflammatory gene expression in the brain that normally occurs during EAE , including the early increase in RANTES:__entity__ ( regulated:__entity__ on:__entity__ activation:__entity__ of:__entity__ normal:__entity__ T-cell:__entity__ expressed:__entity__ and:__entity__ secreted:__entity__ ) expression , and the later expression of the inducible form of nitric:__entity__ oxide:__entity__ synthase:__entity__ .
The early activation of transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ NF-kappaB:__entity__ was also blocked by the HSR .
The finding that the SR reduces inflammation in the brain and the clinical severity of EAE opens a novel therapeutic approach for prevention of autoimmune diseases .
In vivo detection of intracellular signaling pathways in developing thymocytes .
Information regarding the intracellular signaling processes that occur during the development of T cells has largely been obtained with the use of transgenic mouse models , which although providing invaluable information are time consuming and costly .
To this end , we have developed a novel system that facilitates the in vivo analysis of signal transduction pathways during T-lymphocyte development .
This approach uses reporter-plasmids:__entity__ for the detection of intracellular signals mediated by the mitogen-activated:__entity__ protein:__entity__ kinase:__entity__ or cyclic:__entity__ AMP-dependent:__entity__ protein:__entity__ kinase:__entity__ .
Reporter-plasmids:__entity__ are transfected into thymocytes in fetal thymic organ culture by accelerated DNA/particle bombardment ( gene gun ) , and the activation of a signaling pathway is determined in the form of a standard luciferase assay .
Importantly , this powerful technique preserves the structural integrity of the thymus , and will provide an invaluable tool to study how thymocytes respond to normal environmental stimuli encountered during differentiation within the thymic milieu .
Thus , this method allows for the monitoring of signals that occur in a biological time frame , such as during differentiation , and within the natural environment of differentiating cells .

Oxidized alkyl phospholipids are specific , high affinity peroxisome proliferator-activated receptor gamma ligands and agonists .
Synthetic high affinity peroxisome proliferator-activated receptor ( PPAR ) agonists are known , but biologic ligands are of low affinity .

[ ( 3 ) H ] azPC bound recombinant:__entity__ PPARgamma:__entity__ with an affinity ( K ( d ) ( ( app ) ) approximately 40 nm ) that was equivalent to rosiglitazone ( BRL49653 ) , and competition with rosiglitazone showed that binding occurred in the ligand-binding:__entity__ pocket:__entity__ .
azPC induced PPRE reporter gene expression , as did rosiglitazone , with a half-maximal effect at 100 nm .

The scavenger:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ CD36:__entity__ is encoded by a PPRE-responsive:__entity__ gene:__entity__ , and azPC enhanced expression of CD36:__entity__ in primary human monocytes .

Results with a small molecule phospholipid:__entity__ flippase:__entity__ mimetic:__entity__ suggest azPC acts intracellularly and that cellular azPC accumulation was efficient .

Molecular pathogenesis of influenza A virus infection and virus-induced regulation of cytokine:__entity__ gene:__entity__ expression .
Despite vaccines and antiviral substances influenza still causes significant morbidity and mortality world wide .
Better understanding of the molecular mechanisms of influenza virus replication , pathogenesis and host immune responses is required for the development of more efficient means of prevention and treatment of influenza .
Influenza A virus , which replicates in epithelial cells and leukocytes , regulates host cell transcriptional and translational systems and activates , as well as downregulates apoptotic pathways .
Influenza A virus infection results in the production of chemotactic ( RANTES:__entity__ , MIP-1:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ , MCP-1:__entity__ , MCP-3:__entity__ , and IP-10:__entity__ ) , pro-inflammatory ( IL-1:__entity__ beta:__entity__ , IL-6:__entity__ , IL-18:__entity__ , and TNF-alpha:__entity__ ) , and antiviral:__entity__ (:__entity__ IFN-alpha/beta:__entity__ ):__entity__ cytokines:__entity__ .

Comparison of hprt and lacI mutant frequency with DNA adduct formation in N-hydroxy-2-acetylaminofluorene-treated Big Blue rats .
N-Hydroxy-2-acetylaminofluorene ( N-OH-AAF ) is the proximate carcinogenic metabolite of the powerful rat liver carcinogen 2-acetylaminofluorene .
In this study , transgenic Big Blue ( R ) rats were used to examine the relationship between in vivo mutagenicity and DNA adduct formation by N-OH-AAF in the target liver compared with that in nontarget tissues .
Male rats were given one , two , or four doses of 25 mg N-OH-AAF/kg body weight by i.p. injection at 4-day intervals , and groups of treated and control rats were euthanized up to 10 weeks after beginning the dosing .
Mutant frequencies were measured in the spleen:__entity__ lymphocyte:__entity__ hprt:__entity__ gene:__entity__ , and lacI mutant frequencies were determined in the liver and spleen lymphocytes .
At 6 weeks after beginning the dosing , the hprt mutant frequency in spleen lymphocytes from the four-dose group was 16.5 x 10 ( -6 ) compared with 3.2 x 10 ( -6 ) in control animals .
Also at 6 weeks , rats given one , two , or four doses of N-OH-AAF had lacI mutant frequencies in the liver of 97.6 , 155.6 , and 406.8 x 10 ( -6 ) , respectively , compared with a control frequency of 25.7 x 10 ( -6 ) ; rats given four doses had lacI mutant frequencies in spleen lymphocytes of 55.8 x 10 ( -6 ) compared with a control frequency of 20.4 x 10 ( -6 ) .
Additional rats were evaluated for DNA adduct formation in the liver , spleen lymphocytes , and bone marrow by ( 32 ) P-postlabeling .
Adduct analysis was conducted 1 day after one , two , and four treatments with N-OH-AAF , 5 days after one treatment , and 9 days after two treatments .
N- ( Deoxyguanosin-8-yl ) -2-aminofluorene was the major DNA adduct identified in all the tissues examined .
Adduct concentrations increased with total dose to maximum values in samples taken 1 day after two doses , and remained essentially the same after four doses .
In samples taken after four doses , adduct levels were 103 , 28 , and 7 fmol/microg of DNA in liver , spleen lymphocytes , and bone marrow , respectively .
The results indicate that the extent of both DNA adduct formation and mutant induction correlates with the organ specificity for N-OH-AAF carcinogenesis in the rat .

Gene transfer of antisense hypoxia:__entity__ inducible:__entity__ factor-1:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ enhances the therapeutic efficacy of cancer immunotherapy .
Solid tumors meet their demands for nascent blood vessels and increased glycolysis , to combat hypoxia , by activating multiple genes involved in angiogenesis and glucose metabolism .
Hypoxia:__entity__ inducible:__entity__ factor-1:__entity__ ( HIF-1:__entity__ ) is a constitutively expressed basic helix-loop-helix:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ , formed by the assembly of HIF-1alpha:__entity__ and HIF-1beta:__entity__ ( Arnt:__entity__ ) , that is stablized in response to hypoxia , and rapidly degraded under normoxic conditions .

Analysis of BCL-6 mutations in classic Hodgkin disease of the B- and T-cell type .

Furthermore , hematopoiesis in mice lacking Gadd45gamma:__entity__ is not impaired and Gadd45gamma:__entity__ -deficient T lymphocytes show normal responses to IL-2:__entity__ .
These data demonstrate that Gadd45gamma:__entity__ is not essential for normal mouse development and hematopoiesis , possibly due to functional redundancy among the Gadd45:__entity__ family:__entity__ members:__entity__ .
Gadd45gamma:__entity__ is also dispensable for IL-2:__entity__ -induced T-cell proliferation .

Immunohistochemical detection of interferon-gamma-producing cells in dermatophytosis .
Skin lesions of dermatophytosis are thought to be a result of a T cell -dependent inflammatory response that is mediated by various cytokines:__entity__ .
We examined whether IFN-gamma-positive cells ( as expression of Th1 response ) were present in the skin lesions of dermatophytosis in situ by immunohistochemical techniques .
Mixtures of CD4-positive T cells and CD8-positive T cells were found to be present in the dermal infiltrates of the lesions .
Considerable numbers of CD1a-positive cells were detected in the upper dermis and epidermis .
A marked accumulation of CD68-positive cells was found in the upper dermis .
IFN-gamma-positive cells were present in the upper dermis of the lesions .
The pattern of IFN-gamma:__entity__ staining appeared to be intracellular in mononuclear lymphoid cells .
The staining was considered to be highly specific because it could be completely blocked by preabsorption with recombinant:__entity__ IFN-gamma:__entity__ .
Our data support the hypothesis that the skin lesions of dermatophytosis may be associated with a Th1 response .
Th1 response , which is characterized by IFN-gamma:__entity__ release , is thought to be involved in the host defense against dermatophytes and to reflect cutaneous reaction in dermatophytosis .

Retinoic acid up-regulates myeloid ICAM-3 expression and function in a cell-specific fashion -- evidence for retinoid signaling pathways in the mast cell lineage .
Investigation of mast cell responsiveness toward retinoic acid ( RA ) revealed selective promotion of ICAM-3:__entity__ expression in the human mast cell line HMC-1 .

CD28:__entity__ and T cell co-stimulation .
Over the last decade the concept of T cell co-stimulation has emerged to take a central role in the process of T cell activation .
However , the exact definition of co-stimulation is still unclear .
In this review , we re-examine the concept of co-stimulation .
We suggest that while co-stimulation is important , there is little evidence to link co-stimulation with T cell anergy .
We then suggest a framework for studying co-stimulation .
Focusing on recent advances in our understanding of CD28:__entity__ , we discuss four areas of T cell activation where co-stimulation may play a role .

Tolerance develops in these mice .

In contrast to CD8 ( + ) Des ( + ) T cells activated in vivo with APCs , which express high AP-1:__entity__ and high NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ transcriptional activity , the unresponsive CD8 ( + ) Des ( + ) T cells expressed no AP-1:__entity__ and only weak NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ transcriptional activity .
The differences in NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ transcriptional activity correlated with the generation of distinct NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ complexes:__entity__ .
Indeed , in vivo primed T cells predominantly express p50/p50:__entity__ and:__entity__ p65/p50:__entity__ dimers:__entity__ , whereas these p50-containing:__entity__ complexes:__entity__ are barely detectable in tolerant T cells that express p65-:__entity__ and:__entity__ c-Rel-containing:__entity__ complexes:__entity__ .
These observations suggest that fine regulation of NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ complex:__entity__ formation may determine T cell fate .
Transcriptional regulation in lymphocytes .
Lymphocytes have been used to investigate many cellular processes , including lineage commitment , differentiation , proliferation and apoptosis .
The transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ that mediate these processes are often expressed broadly in many cell types .
The emerging theme is one of cell-type-specific regulation , affecting not only the functional activation of transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ but also their access to appropriate regions of DNA .

An instructive component in T helper cell type 2 ( Th2 ) development mediated by GATA-3:__entity__ .
Although interleukin:__entity__ (:__entity__ IL:__entity__ ):__entity__ -12:__entity__ and IL-4:__entity__ polarize naive CD4 ( + ) T cells toward T helper cell type 1 ( Th1 ) or Th2 phenotypes , it is not known whether cytokines:__entity__ instruct the developmental fate in uncommitted progenitors or select for outgrowth of cells that have stochastically committed to a particular fate .
To distinguish these instructive and selective models , we used surface affinity matrix technology to isolate committed progenitors based on cytokine secretion phenotype and developed retroviral-based tagging approaches to directly monitor individual progenitor fate decisions at the clonal and population levels .
We observe IL-4:__entity__ -dependent redirection of phenotype in cells that have already committed to a non-IL-4-producing fate , inconsistent with predictions of the selective model .
Further , retroviral tagging of naive progenitors with the Th2-specific:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ GATA-3:__entity__ provided direct evidence for instructive differentiation , and no evidence for the selective outgrowth of cells committed to either the Th1 or Th2 fate .
These data would seem to exclude selection as an exclusive mechanism in Th1 / Th2 differentiation , and support an instructive model of cytokine-driven transcriptional programming of cell fate decisions .

Mechanism of the inhibitory effect of protease inhibitor on tumor:__entity__ necrosis:__entity__ factor:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ production of monocytes .

Homocysteine stimulates the expression of monocyte:__entity__ chemoattractant:__entity__ protein-1:__entity__ in endothelial cells leading to enhanced monocyte chemotaxis .

In conclusion , our results indicate that homocysteine stimulates MCP-1:__entity__ expression in endothelial cells leading to enhanced monocyte chemotaxis .
Inducible resistance to Fas-mediated apoptosis in B cells .
Apoptosis produced in B cells through Fas:__entity__ ( APO-1:__entity__ , CD95:__entity__ ) triggering is regulated by signals derived from other surface receptors : CD40 engagement produces upregulation of Fas:__entity__ expression and marked susceptibility to Fas:__entity__ -induced cell death , whereas antigen receptor engagement , or IL-4R engagement , inhibits Fas:__entity__ killing and in so doing induces a state of Fas:__entity__ -resistance , even in otherwise sensitive , CD40:__entity__ -stimulated targets .
Surface:__entity__ immunoglobulin:__entity__ and IL-4R:__entity__ utilize at least partially distinct pathways to produce Fas:__entity__ -resistance that differentially depend on PKC:__entity__ and STAT6:__entity__ , respectively .
Further , surface immunoglobulin signaling for inducible Fas:__entity__ -resistance bypasses Btk:__entity__ , requires NF-kappaB:__entity__ , and entails new macromolecular synthesis .
Terminal effectors of B cell Fas:__entity__ -resistance include the known anti-apoptotic:__entity__ gene:__entity__ products:__entity__ , Bcl-xL:__entity__ and FLIP:__entity__ , and a novel anti-apoptotic:__entity__ gene:__entity__ that encodes FAIM:__entity__ ( Fas:__entity__ Apoptosis:__entity__ Inhibitory:__entity__ Molecule:__entity__ ) .
faim:__entity__ was identified by differential display and exists in two alternatively spliced forms ; faim-S:__entity__ is broadly expressed , but faim-L expression is tissue-specific .
The FAIM:__entity__ sequence:__entity__ is highly evolu- tionarily conserved , suggesting an important role for this molecule throughout phylogeny .
Inducible resistance to Fas:__entity__ killing is hypothesized to protect foreign antigen-specific B cells during potentially hazardous interactions with FasL-bearing T cells , whereas autoreactive B cells fail to become Fas:__entity__ -resistant and are deleted via Fas:__entity__ -dependent cytotoxicity .
Inadvertent or aberrant acquisition of Fas:__entity__ -resistance may permit autoreactive B cells to escape Fas:__entity__ deletion , and malignant lymphocytes to impede anti-tumor immunity .
Stromal:__entity__ cell-derived:__entity__ factor:__entity__ 1:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ -induced chemotaxis in T cells is mediated by nitric oxide signaling pathways .
Stromal:__entity__ cell-derived:__entity__ factor:__entity__ 1:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ ( SDF1:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ ) and its cognate chemokine:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ CXCR4:__entity__ act as potent chemoattractants and regulate trafficking and homing of hematopoietic progenitor cells and lymphocytes .

The lack of NF-kappa B transactivation and PKC epsilon expression in CD4 ( + ) CD8 ( + ) thymocytes correlates with negative selection .

CD2 stimulation leads to the delayed and prolonged activation of STAT1:__entity__ in T cells but not NK cells .
OBJECTIVE : T lymphocytes can be activated by soluble factors such as cytokines:__entity__ or through direct cell-cell interactions .
Although cytokine:__entity__ receptors:__entity__ are known to signal through STAT:__entity__ family:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ , the mechanisms by which other cell-surface:__entity__ molecules:__entity__ , such as CD2:__entity__ , transduce signals is unclear .
The goal of this study was to determine whether stimulation of T cells through CD2:__entity__ recapitulates aspects of cytokine:__entity__ -induced T-cell activation by use of STAT:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ .
MATERIALS AND METHODS : T cells were treated with anti-CD2:__entity__ antibodies:__entity__ or cells bearing the natural CD2:__entity__ ligand:__entity__ CD58:__entity__ , after which signaling through STAT:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ was assessed .
RESULTS : Stimulation of CD2:__entity__ on primary T lymphocytes leads to the tyrosine phosphorylation , nuclear translocation , and DNA binding of STAT1:__entity__ .
In contrast to stimulation by cytokines:__entity__ , the activation of STAT1:__entity__ in response to CD2 ligation is delayed and does not involve Jak:__entity__ kinases:__entity__ .
Furthermore , while STAT phosphorylation induced by cytokines:__entity__ is generally transient , STAT1 phosphorylation following CD2 stimulation persists for a period of days .
Transcription of key target genes such as IRF1:__entity__ and c-fos:__entity__ proceeds with delayed kinetics following CD2 stimulation , suggesting that this unique pattern of STAT activation may lead to a distinct cellular response following CD2 ligation .
This pathway appears to be restricted to T cells , as stimulation of CD2:__entity__ on NK cells does not lead to STAT1 activation .
CONCLUSION : Stimulation of T cells through cell-surface:__entity__ molecules:__entity__ such as CD2:__entity__ involves activation of STAT:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ , thus recapitulating elements of cytokine signaling .
NFATc1:__entity__ and NFATc2:__entity__ together control both T and B cell activation and differentiation .
NFAT:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ play critical roles in gene transcription during immune responses .
To investigate further the two most prominent NFAT:__entity__ family:__entity__ members:__entity__ , NFATc1:__entity__ and NFATc2:__entity__ , we generated mice bearing lymphoid systems devoid of both .
Doubly deficient T cells displayed cell surface markers of activation yet were significantly deficient in the development of multiple effector functions , including Th:__entity__ cytokine:__entity__ production , surface:__entity__ effector:__entity__ molecule:__entity__ expression , and cytolytic activity .
Nevertheless , doubly deficient B cells were hyperactivated , as evidenced by extremely elevated serum IgG1:__entity__ and IgE:__entity__ , as well as plasma cell expansion and infiltration of end organs .
Thus , in T cells , NFATc1:__entity__ and NFATc2:__entity__ are dispensable for inflammatory reactivity but are required for effector differentiation , while in B cells , NFATs:__entity__ regulate both normal homeostasis and differentiation .
Epstein-barr virus immediate-early:__entity__ protein:__entity__ BZLF1:__entity__ is SUMO-1 modified and disrupts promyelocytic leukemia bodies .
Although the immediate-early:__entity__ proteins:__entity__ of both herpes simplex virus ( HSV ) and cytomegalovirus ( CMV ) are known to modify promyelocytic leukemia ( PML ) ( ND10 ) bodies in the nucleus of the host cell , it has been unclear whether lytic infection with gamma herpesviruses induces a similar effect .
The PML:__entity__ protein:__entity__ is induced by interferon:__entity__ , involved in major:__entity__ histocompatibility:__entity__ complex:__entity__ class:__entity__ I:__entity__ presentation , and necessary for certain types of apoptosis .
Therefore , it is likely that PML bodies function in an antiviral capacity .
SUMO-1 modification of PML:__entity__ is known to be required for the formation of PML bodies .
To examine whether Epstein-Barr virus ( EBV ) lytic replication interferes with PML bodies , we expressed the EBV:__entity__ immediate-early:__entity__ genes:__entity__ BZLF1:__entity__ (:__entity__ Z:__entity__ ):__entity__ and BRLF1:__entity__ (:__entity__ R:__entity__ ):__entity__ in EBV-positive cell lines and examined PML:__entity__ localization .
Both Z and R expression resulted in PML:__entity__ dispersion in EBV-positive cells .
Z but not R expression is sufficient to disrupt PML bodies in EBV-negative cell lines .
We show that dispersion of PML bodies by Z:__entity__ requires a portion of the transcriptional:__entity__ activation:__entity__ domain:__entity__ of Z:__entity__ but not the DNA-binding function .

Granulocytic differentiation of human NB4 promyelocytic leukemia cells induced by all-trans retinoic acid metabolites .
The metabolism of all-trans retinoic acid ( ATRA ) has been reported to be partly responsible for the in vivo resistance to ATRA seen in the treatment of human acute promyelocytic leukemia ( APL ) .
However , ATRA metabolism appears to be involved in the growth inhibition of several cancer cell lines in vitro .
The purpose of this study was to evaluate the in vitro activity of the principal metabolites of ATRA [ 4-hydroxy-retinoic acid ( 4-OH-RA ) , 18-hydroxy-retinoic acid ( 18-OH-RA ) , 4-oxo-retinoic acid ( 4-oxo-RA ) , and 5 , 6-epoxy-retinoic acid ( 5 , 6-epoxy-RA ) ] in NB4 , a human promyelocytic leukemia cell line that exhibits the APL diagnostic t ( 15 ; 17 ) chromosomal translocation and expresses the PML-RAR:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ fusion:__entity__ protein:__entity__ .
We established that the four ATRA metabolites were indeed formed by the NB4 cells in vitro .
NB4 cell growth was inhibited ( 69-78 % at 120 h ) and cell cycle progression in the G1 phase ( 82-85 % at 120 h ) was blocked by ATRA and all of the metabolites at 1 microM concentration .
ATRA and its metabolites could induce NB4 cells differentiation with similar activity , as evaluated by cell morphology , by the nitroblue tetrazolium reduction test ( 82-88 % at 120 h ) or by the expression of the maturation:__entity__ specific:__entity__ cell:__entity__ surface:__entity__ marker:__entity__ CD11c:__entity__ .
In addition , nuclear body reorganization to macropunctated structures , as well as the degradation of PML-RAR:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ , was found to be similar for ATRA and all of its metabolites .
Comparison of the relative potency of the retinoids using the nitroblue tetrazolium reduction test showed effective concentrations required to differentiate 50 % of cells in 72 h as follows : ATRA , 15.8 +/- 1.7 nM ; 4-oxo-RA , 38.3 +/- 1.3 nM ; 18-OH-RA , 55.5 +/- 1.8 nM ; 4-OH-RA , 79.8 +/- 1.8 nM ; and 5 , 6-epoxy-RA , 99.5 +/- 1.5 nM .
The ATRA metabolites were found to exert their differentiation effects via the RAR:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ nuclear:__entity__ receptors:__entity__ , because the RAR alpha-specific antagonist BMS614 blocked metabolite-induced CD11c expression in NB4 cells .
These data demonstrate that the principal ATRA Phase 1 metabolites can elicit leukemia cell growth inhibition and differentiation in vitro through the RAR alpha signaling pathway , and they suggest that these metabolites may play a role in ATRA antileukemic activity in vivo .
Expression of oestrogen:__entity__ and:__entity__ progesterone:__entity__ receptors:__entity__ by mast cells alone , but not lymphocytes , macrophages or other immune cells in human upper airways .
BACKGROUND : Nasal polyposis often coexists with asthma in airway inflammatory conditions characterised by the infiltration of a range of immune cells .
A potentially important role for ovarian hormones has been implicated in airway inflammation but the cellular target for such action is not known .
METHODS : Expression of oestrogen:__entity__ receptors:__entity__ ( ER:__entity__ ) and progesterone:__entity__ receptors:__entity__ ( PR:__entity__ ) was examined using immunohistochemistry in formalin fixed nasal polyp tissues from 47 subjects .

The frequencies for expression were 61.7 % for ER positive and 59.6 % for PR positive cells .
The expression of ER:__entity__ / PR:__entity__ was independent of patient sex and age but was highly correlated with the numbers of mast cells ( r = 0.973 , p < 0.001 for ER:__entity__ ; r = 0.955 , p < 0.001 for PR:__entity__ ) .
Fewer than 5 % of mast cells were found to be negative for ER:__entity__ / PR:__entity__ expression .
CONCLUSIONS : Mast cells alone , but not lymphocytes , macrophages , or other immune cells , express ER:__entity__ / PR:__entity__ in human upper airways .
Numerous ER/PR positive mast cells exist in nasal polyps , indicating that this may be a major route for the involvement of sex hormones in airway inflammation when exposed to the higher and varying concentration of oestrogen and progesterone characteristic of females .

Induction of apoptosis in human lymphocytes by the herbicide 2 , 4-dichlorophenoxyacetic acid .
Dimethylammonium salt of 2 , 4-dichlorophenoxyacetic acid ( DMA-2 , 4-D ) is a widely used herbicide that is considered moderately toxic .
In the present study we found that DMA-2 , 4-D is able to cause apoptosis in peripheral blood lymphocytes of healthy individuals and Jurkat T cells .
Apoptosis induced by DMA-2 , 4-D was dose and time dependent , independent of Fas:__entity__ , TNF:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ 1:__entity__ or the aromatic:__entity__ hydrocarbon:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ , and involved disruption of the mitochondrial transmembrane potential and activation of caspase-9:__entity__ .
ZVAD-FMK , a broad-spectrum inhibitor of caspases:__entity__ , blocked DMA-2 , 4-D-induced apoptosis completely .
While an inhibitor of caspase-9:__entity__ , as well as caspase-9:__entity__ and caspase-3 inhibitors in combination , strongly blocked DMA-2 , 4-D-induced apoptosis , an inhibitor of caspase-3:__entity__ had a moderate inhibitory effect .
Unlike Fas:__entity__ -mediated apoptosis , the initiator:__entity__ caspase:__entity__ , caspase-8:__entity__ , was not involved in DMA-2 , 4-D-induced apoptosis .
Transfection of Jurkat cells with Bcl-2:__entity__ prevented DMA-2 , 4-D-induced disruption of the mitochondrial transmembrane potential and led to a complete blockage of apoptosis .
Our data indicate that DMA-2 , 4-D kills human lymphocytes by initiating apoptosis via a direct effect on mitochondria .
The activation of caspases:__entity__ occurs downstream of mitochondrial damage , and the dysfunction of mitochondria appears to be sufficient for triggering all downstream events leading to apoptosis .

Selective inhibition of interleukin-4 gene expression in human T cells by aspirin .
Previous studies indicated that aspirin ( acetylsalicylic acid [ ASA ] ) can have profound immunomodulatory effects by regulating cytokine gene expression in several types of cells .
This study is the first in which concentrations of ASA in the therapeutic range were found to significantly reduce interleukin:__entity__ (:__entity__ IL:__entity__ ):__entity__ -4:__entity__ secretion and RNA expression in freshly isolated and mitogen-primed human CD4+ T cells .
In contrast , ASA did not affect IL-13:__entity__ , interferon-gamma:__entity__ , and IL-2:__entity__ expression .
ASA inhibited IL-4:__entity__ , but not IL-2:__entity__ , promoter-driven chloramphenicol acetyltransferase expression in transiently transfected Jurkat T cells .
The structurally unrelated nonsteroidal anti-inflammatory drugs indomethacin and flurbiprofen did not affect cytokine gene expression in T cells , whereas the weak cyclo-oxygenase inhibitor salicylic acid was at least as effective as ASA in inhibiting IL-4:__entity__ expression and promoter activity .
The inhibitory effect of ASA on IL-4 transcription was not mediated by decreased nuclear expression of the known salicylate:__entity__ target:__entity__ nuclear:__entity__ factor:__entity__ (:__entity__ NF:__entity__ ):__entity__ -kappaB:__entity__ and was accompanied by reduced binding of an inducible factor to an IL-4:__entity__ promoter:__entity__ region:__entity__ upstream of , but not overlapping , the NF:__entity__ of:__entity__ activated:__entity__ T:__entity__ cells-:__entity__ and:__entity__ NF-kappaB-binding:__entity__ P1:__entity__ element:__entity__ .
It is concluded that anti-inflammatory salicylates , by means of a previously unrecognized mechanism of action , can influence the nature of adaptive immune responses by selectively inhibiting the expression of IL-4:__entity__ , a critical effector of these responses , in CD4+ T cells .
Molecular and cellular mediators of interleukin-1:__entity__ -dependent acute inflammatory arthritis .

IL-1:__entity__ contributes to leukocyte recruitment to the synovium and directly induces chemokine mRNA production by synovial cells .
This model of acute monarticular arthritis is particularly suitable for further investigations into cell-mediated immunity in arthritis and the role of IL-1:__entity__ .
Positive and negative regulation of granulopoiesis by endogenous:__entity__ RARalpha:__entity__ .
Acute promyelocytic leukemia ( APL ) is always associated with chromosomal translocations that disrupt the retinoic:__entity__ acid:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ (:__entity__ RARalpha:__entity__ ):__entity__ gene:__entity__ .
Whether these translocations relate to a role for endogenous:__entity__ RARalpha:__entity__ in normal granulopoiesis remains uncertain because most studies addressing this question have used non-physiological overexpression systems .
Granulocyte differentiation in cells derived from RARalpha-deficient ( RARalpha ( -/- ) ) mice was studied and evaluated in the context of agonist-bound:__entity__ and:__entity__ ligand-free:__entity__ RARalpha:__entity__ .
Our results demonstrate that RARalpha:__entity__ is dispensable for granulopoiesis , as RARalpha ( -/- ) mice have a normal granulocyte population despite an impaired ability to respond to retinoids .
However , although it is not absolutely required , RARalpha:__entity__ can bidirectionally modulate granulopoiesis .
RARalpha:__entity__ stimulates differentiation in response to exogenous retinoic acid .
Furthermore , endogenous retinoids control granulopoiesis in vivo , as either vitamin A-deficient mice or animals treated with an RAR antagonist accumulate more immature granulocytes in their bone marrow .
Conversely , RARalpha:__entity__ acts to limit differentiation in the absence of ligand:__entity__ because granulocyte precursors from RARalpha ( -/- ) mice differentiate earlier in culture .
Thus , the block in granulopoiesis exerted by RARalpha:__entity__ fusion:__entity__ proteins:__entity__ expressed in APL cells may correspond to an amplification of a normal function of unliganded:__entity__ RARalpha:__entity__ .

Distal promoter activity is maintained throughout T cell development and at lower levels in B cell development , but downregulated in natural killer cell development .
The distal:__entity__ N-terminal:__entity__ isoform:__entity__ binds to functionally important regulatory:__entity__ sites:__entity__ from known target:__entity__ genes:__entity__ with two- to threefold higher affinity than the proximal:__entity__ N-terminal:__entity__ isoform:__entity__ .

Constitutive PI3-K activity is essential for proliferation , but not survival , of Theileria parva-transformed B cells .
Theileria is an intracellular parasite that causes lymphoproliferative disorders in cattle , and infection of leucocytes induces a transformed phenotype similar to tumour cells , but the mechanisms by which the parasite induces this phenotype are not understood .
Here , we show that infected B lymphocytes display constitutive phosphoinositide 3-kinase ( PI3-K ) activity , which appears to be necessary for proliferation , but not survival .
Importantly , we demonstrate that one mechanism by which PI3-K:__entity__ mediates the proliferation of infected B lymphocytes is through the induction of a granulocyte-monocyte:__entity__ colony-stimulating:__entity__ factor:__entity__ ( GM-CSF:__entity__ ) -dependent autocrine loop .
PI3-K:__entity__ induction of GM-CSF:__entity__ appears to be at the transcriptional level and , consistently , we demonstrate that PI3-K:__entity__ is also involved in the constitutive induction of AP-1:__entity__ and NF-kappaB:__entity__ , which characterizes Theileria-infected leucocytes .
Taken together , our results highlight a novel strategy exploited by the intracellular parasite Theileria to induce continued proliferation of its host leucocyte .
Lymphokine:__entity__ dependence of STAT3 activation produced by surface immunoglobulin cross-linking and by phorbol ester plus calcium ionophore treatment in B cells .
Stimulation of B cells by surface:__entity__ immunoglobulin:__entity__ ( sIg:__entity__ ) triggering , or through the mitogenic combination of phorbol ester and calcium ionophore , is accompanied by activation of STAT:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factors:__entity__ .
The mechanism responsible for the delayed nuclear accumulation of phosphorylated:__entity__ STAT3:__entity__ was examined in detail , focusing on the role of B:__entity__ cell-derived:__entity__ lymphokines:__entity__ .
sIg:__entity__ -induced activation of STAT3:__entity__ was partially inhibited in B cells obtained from IL-6- or IL-10-deficient mice , and was partially blocked by neutralizing:__entity__ antibodies:__entity__ directed against either of these lymphokines:__entity__ .
sIg:__entity__ -induced STAT3 activation was completely inhibited by combining IL-6-:__entity__ and:__entity__ IL-10-specific:__entity__ neutralizing:__entity__ antibodies:__entity__ , or by adding individual neutralizing:__entity__ antibodies:__entity__ to B cells obtained from lymphokine-deficient animals .
In contrast , IL-10:__entity__ alone appeared to account for STAT3 activation resulting from B cell stimulation with phorbol ester and calcium ionophore .
In keeping with these results , soluble IL-6:__entity__ and IL-10:__entity__ were found in supernatant fluid obtained from stimulated B cells .
This work indicates that a lymphokine pathway is responsible for STAT3 activation that occurs late after B cell stimulation , and points out differences in B cell activation that result from stimulation through the antigen:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ and through pharmacological mimicry of signaling:__entity__ mediators:__entity__ .
Transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ AP-4:__entity__ is a ligand:__entity__ for immunoglobulin-kappa:__entity__ promoter:__entity__ E-box:__entity__ elements:__entity__ .
Immunoglobulin:__entity__ (:__entity__ Ig:__entity__ ):__entity__ -kappa:__entity__ promoters:__entity__ from humans and mice share conserved:__entity__ sequences:__entity__ .
The octamer:__entity__ element:__entity__ is common to all Ig:__entity__ promoters:__entity__ and pivotal for their function .

One example is an E-box:__entity__ of the E47/E12:__entity__ type:__entity__ (:__entity__ 5'-CAGCTG-3:__entity__ ':__entity__ ):__entity__ , which is found in all promoters of the human:__entity__ and:__entity__ murine:__entity__ Ig-kappa:__entity__ gene:__entity__ subgroups/families:__entity__ , with the exception of subgroups II and VI and their related murine:__entity__ families:__entity__ .

Based on these data , and the conservation of the 5'-CAGCTG-3:__entity__ ':__entity__ motif:__entity__ among human:__entity__ and:__entity__ murine:__entity__ kappa:__entity__ promoters:__entity__ , we propose that AP-4:__entity__ is the major:__entity__ ligand:__entity__ for Ig-kappa:__entity__ promoter:__entity__ E-boxes:__entity__ .
A 16-mer peptide ( RQIKIWFQNRRMKWKK ) from antennapedia preferentially targets the Class I pathway .
Translocation of antigenic peptides into the cytosol of antigen presenting cells facilitates proteosomal processing and loading into Class:__entity__ I:__entity__ molecules:__entity__ for MHC presentation on the cell surface .

Bone marrow cells promote TH2 polarization and inhibit virus-specific CTL generation .
This laboratory recently reported that human bone marrow cells ( BMC ) inhibit the generation of virus-specific CTL in culture .
The culture supernatants contained increased levels of prostaglandin:__entity__ E:__entity__ (:__entity__ 2:__entity__ ):__entity__ (:__entity__ PGE:__entity__ (:__entity__ 2:__entity__ ):__entity__ ):__entity__ ( shown to favor TH2 cell development ) and also inhibited EBV-CTL effector cell development .
In this study , we obtained PBL from Epstein-Barr virus ( EBV ) IgG:__entity__ antibody:__entity__ positive kidney transplant recipients ( R ) and their living-related donors ( LRD ) one year after renal transplantation .

Inhibition was even observed by preparing EBV-CTL generating cultures in trans-wells that separated the autologous BMC from the PBL + EBV-B .
It was then observed that CD3+ cells obtained after 7 days of culture in the presence of autologous BMC could be used as inhibitors of EBV-CTL generation .
Protein:__entity__ Kinase:__entity__ A:__entity__ ( PKA:__entity__ ) , a cAMP:__entity__ kinase:__entity__ that is involved in the upregulation of TH2:__entity__ cytokine:__entity__ activity , was increased in EBV-CTL cultures by the presence of BMC .

These results show that the BMC inhibition is mediated by soluble:__entity__ factors:__entity__ ( cytokines:__entity__ ) and that cell-cell contact in this autologous system is not required , so that BMC ( at least partially , via cytokine production ) promote TH2 polarization in culture .
Moreover , TH2 cells induced by culturing with autologous BMC directly inhibit EBV-CTL generation , and TH2:__entity__ associated PKA:__entity__ , CCR3:__entity__ , and STAT-6:__entity__ phosphorylation are enhanced by BMC .
Reduction in DNA binding activity of the transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ Pax-5a:__entity__ in B lymphocytes of aged mice .
Aging has been associated with intrinsic changes of the humoral immune response , which may lead to an increased occurrence of autoimmune disorders and pathogenic susceptibility .
The transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ Pax-5:__entity__ is a key regulator of B cell development .
Pax-5a/B:__entity__ cell-specific:__entity__ activator:__entity__ protein:__entity__ and an alternatively:__entity__ spliced:__entity__ isoform:__entity__ ,:__entity__ Pax-5d:__entity__ , may have opposing functions in transcriptional regulation due to the lack of a transactivation:__entity__ domain:__entity__ in Pax-5d:__entity__ .
To study B cell -specific changes that occur during the aging process , we investigated expression patterns of Pax-5a:__entity__ and:__entity__ 5d:__entity__ in mature B cells of young and aged mice .

NF-kappa:__entity__ B/Rel:__entity__ participation in the lymphokine-dependent proliferation of T lymphoid cells .
Proliferative responses of lymphoid cells to IL-2:__entity__ and IL-4:__entity__ depend on activation of the cells , but the mechanism ( s ) by which activation enhances cellular competence to respond to cytokines:__entity__ is not fully understood .
The NF-kappaB/Rel:__entity__ family:__entity__ represents one signal transduction pathway induced during such activation .
We show in this study that inhibition of NF-kappaB:__entity__ through the expression of an IkappaBalpha:__entity__ ( inhibitory:__entity__ protein:__entity__ that dissociates from NF-kappaB:__entity__ ) mutant refractory to signal-induced degradation ( IkappaBalpha:__entity__ (:__entity__ DeltaN:__entity__ ):__entity__ ) interfered with the acquisition of competence to proliferate in response to IL-4:__entity__ as well as IL-2:__entity__ .
