Although treatment of cells with H2O2 alone did not affect the activity of src:__entity__ family:__entity__ kinases:__entity__ , treatment with H2O2 plus vanadate led to activation of the p56lck:__entity__ and:__entity__ p59fyn:__entity__ tyrosine:__entity__ kinases:__entity__ .
The combined inhibition of phosphatases:__entity__ and activation of kinases:__entity__ provides a potent mechanism for the synergistic effects of H2O2 plus vanadate .
Induction of tyrosine phosphorylation by ROI may thus lead to many of the pleiotropic effects of ROI in lymphoid cells , including downstream activation of PLC:__entity__ gamma:__entity__ 1:__entity__ and NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__
Influence of sex:__entity__ hormone:__entity__ binding:__entity__ globulin:__entity__ and serum:__entity__ albumin:__entity__ on the conversion of androstenedione to testosterone by human erythrocytes .
The influence of human:__entity__ serum:__entity__ albumin:__entity__ and sex:__entity__ hormone:__entity__ binding:__entity__ globulin:__entity__ ( SHBG:__entity__ ) on the enzymic conversion of androstenedione to testosterone in human erythrocytes was investigated in vitro .
Total plasma and albumin:__entity__ delayed the conversion rate of androstenedione , while SHBG:__entity__ increased it markedly .
The effect of SHBG:__entity__ was largely abolished by heating to 60 degrees C for 1 h and by saturating its binding sites by DHT .
The effect of both proteins was found to be related to their concentration .
It appears that the binding sites of albumin:__entity__ provide a mechanism for retarding androstenedione uptake by the erythrocytes and that the high binding affinity of SHBG:__entity__ for testosterone facilitates the diffusion of this steroid out of the cell and thus , displaces the chemical equilibrium within the cell .
Glucocorticoids and lymphocytes .
I .
Increased glucocorticoid:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ levels in antigen-stimulated lymphocytes .
Recently a 2- to 3-fold increase in the number of glucocorticoid:__entity__ receptors:__entity__ in human peripheral lymphocytes has been noted after in vitro mitogen stimulation .
Here , we extend these observations to in vivo immunization .
After unilateral immunization of adrenalectomized male rats , a 50 % increase in glucocorticoid receptor sites per cell , determined by binding of dexamethasone , was observed in cell suspensions of homolateral lymph nodes over those from the contralateral nonimmunized side of the same animal .
The association constant for dexamethasone was similar in both groups , as was the stereospecificity for various steroids , the time course of cytoplasmic and nuclear association , and cytoplasmic-to-nuclear translocation .
Despite a 50 % increase in the number of glucocorticoid receptor sites per cell , the cells from the homolateral and controlateral lymph nodes were equally sensitive to the inhibitory effects of dexamethasone , as determined by measurements of the incorporation of radiolabeled precursors of protein , RNA , and DNA , or measurements of in vitro cell survival .
Glucocorticoid receptors and actions in rat thymocytes and immunologically stimulated human peripheral lymphocytes .
After reviewing briefly our earlier studies on glucocorticoid receptors and mechanisms in thymus cells , we have outlined results from the following two areas of current interest in our laboratories : the `` life-cycle '' of glucocorticoid receptors and complexes in thymus cells , and the levels of glucocorticoid receptors and sensitivity in immunologically stimulated human peripheral lymphocytes .
Several of our results on energetics and kinetics of hormone binding to glucocorticoid:__entity__ receptors:__entity__ in rat thymus cells seem to require extension of the simplest model of hormone-receptor transformations in intact cells .
ATP-depletion experiments suggest the existence of a nonbinding form of the receptor ; `` chase '' experiments suggest reaction of hormone directly with nuclear-bound receptor ; experiments on depletion and replenishment of cytoplasmic:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ using cortisol and dexamethasone suggest the existence of at least two subpopulations of nuclear-bound:__entity__ hormone-receptor:__entity__ complex:__entity__ .
We have found that mitogen or immunologic stimulation of human peripheral lymphocytes in culture leads within 24 h or so to a striking increase in the number of glucocorticoid:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ sites per cell .
We believe this increase may be due to partial synchronization of the cell population in a phase of the cell cycle in which receptor content is high .
Contrary to the widely held view that mitogen-stimulated cells become insensitive to glucocorticoids , our experiments show that with respect to inhibition of thymidine and uridine incorporation and glucose uptake , the cells are highly sensitive to dexamethasone at 24 , 48 , and 72 h after stimulation with concanavalin:__entity__ A:__entity__ .
Nuclear glucocorticoid binding in chronic lymphatic leukemia lymphocytes .
A reliable procedure is described for isolating 3H-triamcinolone:__entity__ acetonide:__entity__ (:__entity__ 3H-TA:__entity__ ):__entity__ receptor:__entity__ complexes:__entity__ from purified chronic lymphatic leukemia ( CLL ) lymphocyte nuclei , based on the use of carbobenzoxy-L-phenylalanine ( CBZ-L-phe ) to prevent breakdown of hormone-receptor:__entity__ complexes:__entity__ during extraction of nuclei with 0.6M KCl .
Using this method , specific nuclear glucocorticoid binding was demonstrated in 14/14 patients with untreated CLL .
No correlation was found between levels of nuclear-associated 3H-TA and peripheral white blood cell count or rosetting ability of circulating lymphocytes .
Multiple closely-linked NFAT/octamer:__entity__ and HMG:__entity__ I:__entity__ (:__entity__ Y:__entity__ ):__entity__ binding:__entity__ sites:__entity__ are part of the interleukin-4 promoter .
We show here that the immediate:__entity__ upstream:__entity__ region:__entity__ ( from position -12 to -270 ) of the murine:__entity__ interleukin:__entity__ 4:__entity__ (:__entity__ Il-4:__entity__ ):__entity__ gene:__entity__ harbors a strong cell-type specific transcriptional:__entity__ enhancer:__entity__ .
In T lymphoma cells , the activity of the Il-4:__entity__ promoter/enhancer:__entity__ is stimulated by phorbol esters , Ca++ ionophores and agonists of protein:__entity__ kinase:__entity__ A:__entity__ and inhibited by low doses of the immunosuppressant cyclosporin A .
The Il-4:__entity__ promoter/enhancer:__entity__ is transcriptionally inactive in B lymphoma cells and HeLa cells .
DNase I footprint protection experiments revealed six sites of the Il-4:__entity__ promoter/enhancer:__entity__ to be bound by nuclear:__entity__ proteins:__entity__ from lymphoid and myeloid cells .
Among them are four purine boxes which have been described to be important sequence motifs of the Il-2:__entity__ promoter:__entity__ .
They contain the motif GGAAA and are recognized by the inducible:__entity__ and:__entity__ cyclosporin:__entity__ A-sensitive:__entity__ transcription:__entity__ factor:__entity__ NFAT-1:__entity__ .
Three of the Il-4:__entity__ NFAT-1:__entity__ sites:__entity__ are closely linked to weak binding sites of Octamer:__entity__ factors:__entity__ .
Several purine boxes and an AT-rich:__entity__ protein-binding:__entity__ site:__entity__ of the Il-4 promoter are also recognized by the high:__entity__ mobility:__entity__ group:__entity__ protein:__entity__ HMG:__entity__ I:__entity__ (:__entity__ Y:__entity__ ) .
Whereas the binding of NFAT-1:__entity__ and Octamer:__entity__ factors:__entity__ enhance the activity of the Il-4:__entity__ promoter:__entity__ , the binding of HMG I ( Y ) suppresses its activity and , therefore , appears to be involved in the suppression of Il-4:__entity__ transcription in resting T lymphocytes .
Reversibility of the differentiated state in somatic cells .
Analysis of de novo gene activation in multinucleated heterokaryons has shown that the differentiated state , although stable , is not irreversible , and can be reprogrammed in the presence of appropriate combinations of trans-acting:__entity__ regulatory:__entity__ molecules:__entity__ .
These properties have been exploited to design strategies for identifying novel regulators of cellular differentiation .
Phosphatidylcholine hydrolysis activates NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ and increases human immunodeficiency virus replication in human monocytes and T lymphocytes .
We have tested whether breakdown of phosphatidylcholine ( PC ) initiated by exogenous addition of a PC-specific:__entity__ phospholipase:__entity__ C:__entity__ ( PC-PLC:__entity__ ) from Bacillus cereus or by endogenous overexpression of PC-PLC:__entity__ induces functional activation of NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ and increases human:__entity__ immunodeficiency:__entity__ virus:__entity__ (:__entity__ HIV:__entity__ ):__entity__ enhancer:__entity__ activity .
PC-PLC-activated hydrolysis of PC was found to induce bona fide p50/p65:__entity__ NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ binding activity in three different cell lines of human or murine origin .
No significant changes in the turnover of other cellular phospholipids were detected in PC-PLC-treated cells .
Induction of NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ by PC-PLC:__entity__ did not depend on de novo synthesis of proteins or autocrine secretion of either tumor:__entity__ necrosis:__entity__ factor:__entity__ or interleukin:__entity__ 1:__entity__ .
In human monocytic and lymphoblastoid T-cell lines , induction of NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ by PC-PLC:__entity__ resulted in clear induction of luciferase:__entity__ expression vectors placed under the control of synthetic:__entity__ kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ enhancers:__entity__ or wild type , but not kappa B-mutated , HIV:__entity__ long:__entity__ terminal:__entity__ repeat:__entity__ constructs:__entity__ .
HIV replication was increased by PC-PLC:__entity__ in chronically infected monocytes and T lymphocytes .
NF-kappa B activation promoted by addition of exogenous:__entity__ PC-PLC:__entity__ correlated with an intense production of diacylglycerol .
However , addition of a phosphatidylinositol-specific:__entity__ PLC:__entity__ from B.cereus also induced diacylglycerol but did not activate kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ enhancer-directed:__entity__ vectors:__entity__ .
PC-PLC-induced NF-kappa B activation could not be blocked by a specific inhibitor of phorbol:__entity__ ester-inducible:__entity__ protein:__entity__ kinases:__entity__ C:__entity__ .
These results indicate that a cellular transduction pathway , dependent on specific PC breakdown , is functional in T lymphocytes and monocytes and may be used by various transmembrane receptors to activate HIV transcription through NF-kappa B-dependent induction of the HIV:__entity__ enhancer:__entity__ .
Novel mechanism for inhibition of human T cells by glucocorticoids .
Glucocorticoids inhibit signal transduction through IL-2:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ .
Interaction of IL-2:__entity__ with its high:__entity__ affinity:__entity__ membrane:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ complex:__entity__ ( IL-2R:__entity__ ) present on activated T lymphocytes induces cell proliferation and mediates effector functions .
Glucocorticoids inhibit IL-2:__entity__ production by inhibiting TCR-mediated signal transduction .
We asked whether they also inhibit the action of IL-2:__entity__ by inhibiting signal transduction through IL-2R:__entity__ .
Human peripheral blood T cells , stimulated with PMA for 48 h ( PMA blasts ) , were incubated with IL-2:__entity__ in the presence of incremental dosages of dexamethasone ( Dex ; 10 ( -5 ) -10 ( -9 ) M ) .
Dex inhibited the IL-2-dependent proliferation of PMA blasts in a dose-dependent fashion ( IC50 , 5 x 10 ( -8 ) M ) .
Cell surface expression of IL-2R:__entity__ alpha-:__entity__ and:__entity__ beta-chains:__entity__ as determined by immunofluorescence analysis was not affected by Dex .
In addition , Scatchard plot analysis of 125I-labeled:__entity__ IL-2:__entity__ showed that Dex did not affect the binding of IL-2:__entity__ , thus suggesting that inhibition is due to a postreceptor effect .
Inhibition of T cell proliferation by Dex was associated with decreased IL-2-dependent tyrosine phosphorylation of several intracellular:__entity__ proteins:__entity__ and decreased phosphorylation of the retinoblastoma:__entity__ gene:__entity__ product:__entity__ Rb:__entity__ , a protein essential for controlling the progression of cells through the cell cycle .
IL-2-dependent IL-2R alpha expression in PMA blasts and NF-kB:__entity__ induction in resting human T cells were also inhibited by Dex .
These results demonstrate that glucocorticoids inhibit preactivated T cells by down-regulating signal transduction through IL-2R:__entity__ .
Chronic human immunodeficiency virus type 1 infection stimulates distinct NF-kappa B/rel DNA binding activities in myelomonoblastic cells .
The relationship between human immunodeficiency virus type 1 ( HIV-1 ) infection and the induction of NF-kappa B binding activity was examined in a myeloid cell model of HIV-1 infection derived from the PLB-985 cell line .
Chronic infection of PLB-985 cells led to increased monocyte-specific surface marker expression , increased c-fms gene transcription , and morphological alterations consistent with differentiation along the monocytic pathway .
PLB-IIIB cells displayed a constitutive NF-kappa B-like binding activity that was distinct from that induced by tumor:__entity__ necrosis:__entity__ factor:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ or phorbol 12-myristate 13-acetate treatment of the parental PLB-985 cell line .
This unique DNA binding activity consisted of proteins of 70:__entity__ ,:__entity__ 90:__entity__ ,:__entity__ and:__entity__ 100:__entity__ kDa:__entity__ with a high degree of binding specificity for the NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ site:__entity__ within the PRDII:__entity__ domain:__entity__ of beta:__entity__ interferon:__entity__ .
In this report , we characterize the nature of these proteins and demonstrate that binding of these proteins is also induced following Sendai paramyxovirus infection .
The 70-kDa:__entity__ protein:__entity__ corresponds to the NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ RelA:__entity__ (:__entity__ p65:__entity__ ):__entity__ subunit:__entity__ , which is activated in response to an acute paramyxovirus infection or a chronic HIV-1 infection .
Virus infection does not appear to alter the amount of RelA:__entity__ ( p65:__entity__ ) or NFKB1:__entity__ ( p50:__entity__ ) but rather affects the capacity of I:__entity__ kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ alpha:__entity__ to sequester RelA:__entity__ (:__entity__ p65:__entity__ ):__entity__ , therefore leading to constitutive levels of RelA DNA binding activity and to increased levels of NF-kappa B-dependent gene activity .
The virally induced 90-:__entity__ to:__entity__ 100-kDa:__entity__ proteins:__entity__ have a distinct binding specificity for the PRDII:__entity__ domain:__entity__ and an AT-rich:__entity__ sequence:__entity__ but do not cross-react with NF-kappa B subunit-specific antisera directed against NFKB1:__entity__ ( p105:__entity__ or p50:__entity__ ) , NFKB2:__entity__ ( p100:__entity__ or p52:__entity__ ) , RelA:__entity__ ( p65:__entity__ ) , or c-rel:__entity__ .
DNA binding of the 90-:__entity__ to:__entity__ 100-kDa:__entity__ proteins:__entity__ was not inhibited by recombinant:__entity__ I:__entity__ kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ alpha/MAD-3:__entity__ and was resistant to tryptic digestion , suggesting that these proteins may not be NF-kappa:__entity__ B:__entity__ related:__entity__ .
Transient cotransfection experiments demonstrated that RelA and NFKB1 expression maximally stimulated HIV-1:__entity__ LTR-:__entity__ and:__entity__ NF-kappa:__entity__ B-dependent:__entity__ reporter:__entity__ genes:__entity__ ; differences in NF-kappa B-like binding activity were also reflected in higher constitutive levels of NF-kappa B-regulated gene expression in HIV-1-infected myeloid cells .
Presence of estrogen-binding sites on macrophage-like synoviocytes and CD8+ , CD29+ , CD45RO+ T lymphocytes in normal and rheumatoid synovium .
OBJECTIVE .
To study the presence of estrogen-binding sites ( EBS ) in the synovial tissues of male and female patients with rheumatoid arthritis ( RA ) and in age- and sex-matched healthy controls .
METHODS .
Both type 1 ( high affinity , low binding capacity ) and type 2 ( reduced affinity , higher binding capacity ) EBS were investigated in both soluble and nuclear fractions of homogenized synovial tissue samples by a dextran-coated charcoal method .
To determine what type of synovial cell was positive for EBS , cryosections of synovial tissues were immunostained with a specific monoclonal:__entity__ anti-estrogen:__entity__ receptor:__entity__ antibody:__entity__ ( anti-ER:__entity__ MAb:__entity__ ) using both immunofluorescence and immunoperoxidase techniques .
Double immunostaining with the anti-ER:__entity__ MAb:__entity__ and with specific:__entity__ MAb:__entity__ to detect different macrophage:__entity__ antigens:__entity__ ( Ber-MAC3:__entity__ , MAC387:__entity__ , CD68:__entity__ ) and CD8+ T cell subsets ( CD29+ , CD45RO+ and CD29- , CD45RO- ) was performed .
RESULTS .
Higher affinity EBS were found mostly in nuclear cell fractions of either RA or control synovial tissues ( 28 of the 33 ) .
These EBS were present to a lesser extent in soluble cell fractions ( 11 of the 33 ) .
Immunostaining showed the estrogen receptor-positive cells to be the macrophage-like synoviocytes and the CD8+ , CD29+ T cells both in RA and in control synovial tissues .
Higher nuclear content of EBS was consistent with more intense nuclear staining of synoviocytes and T cells .
CONCLUSION .
It is conceivable that the immunomodulatory activity exerted by estrogens is at least partly mediated through their interaction with EBS that are present on macrophage-like synoviocytes , functioning as antigen-processing and antigen-presenting cells , and on antigen-experienced ( memory ) CD8+ T lymphocytes ( CD29+ , CD45RO+
